       /*Funkcjonalnosc: odczyt z markseen*/
 (function () {
 /**
 * Zwraca tablice widzianych linkow
 */
 function getSeenAnchors() {
 var items, links;
 //ponizsze zabezpieczenie jest po to, bo na zepsutych przegladarkach obsluga localStorage wywoluje wyjatki
 try {
 items = localStorage ? localStorage.getItem('lastSeen') || '' : '';
 links = items.length ? items.split('|') : [];
 } catch (e) {
 ioError = true;
 links = [];
 if (iwa) {
 iwa('trackEvent', 'localStorageProblem', e.name);
 }
 }
 return links;
 }
 //ukrycie !first elementow
 var seen = false ? getSeenAnchors() : [],
 elements = document.querySelectorAll('.big-four .four-li'),
 anchors = document.querySelectorAll('.big-four .four-li a'),
 i;
 [].forEach.call(anchors, function (el, index) {
 el.parentNode.style.display = 'none';
 });
 for (i=0; i< anchors.length; i++) {
 if (seen.indexOf(anchors[i].href) == -1) {
 anchors[i].parentNode.style.display = 'list-item';
 img = anchors[i].querySelector('img');
 img.src = img.dataset['src'];
 break;
 }
 }
 //ukrywam miniatury
 [].forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.exclusive .tiles-thumb'), function (el) {
 el.style.display = 'none';
 });
 }());
      </script>
